                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.1">
                        <label>4.8.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto bhagandarāṇāñ cikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.2">
                        <label>4.8.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pañca bhagandarā vyākhyātāḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.3">
                        <label>4.8.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣv asādhyaḥ śambūkāvarttaḥ śalyanimittaś ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.3a">
                        <label>4.8.3a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śeṣāḥ kṛcchrasādhyāḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.4">
                        <label>4.8.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra bhagandarapiṭakopadrutam āturam apatarppaṇād yena
                        virecanāntenaikādaśavidhenopakrameṇopacaret | apakkvapiṭakaṃ | pakkveṣu
                        copasnigdhamavagāḍhasvinnaṃ śayyāyāṃ saṃveśyārśasamiva yantrayitvā
                        bhagandaram abhis amīkṣya parācīnamarvākcīnaṃ bahirmmukhamantarmukham vā
                        tataḥ prādāyeṣaṇīnnamayitvā śāyasamuddharecchastreṇa | antarmukhañ caivama
                        śakyaṃ yantram praṇidhāya pravāhato bhagandaramaukhamāsādyeṣaṇīn datvā
                        śastram pātayet | āsādya cāgniṃ kṣāraṃ ceti sāmānyaṃ sarvveṣu </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.5">
                        <label>4.8.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣatas tu nānyatare vraṇaṃ kuryād bhiṣak tu śataponake |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatas tāsūparūḍhāsu śeṣā nāḍīrupācaret | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.6">
                        <label>4.8.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gatayo nyonyasaṃbandhā bahvyāś chindyānyanekadhā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         nāḍīranabhis ambaddhā yaś chinaty ekadhā bhiṣak | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.7">
                        <label>4.8.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sa kuryād vivṛtaṃ jantor mmārggaṅ gudavidāraṇaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya ttraṃ vivṛtaṃ mārggam viṇmūtre tu prapadyataḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.8">
                        <label>4.8.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sāṭopaṃ gudaśūlañ ca karoti pavano bhṛśaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāpi śatatamtro 'pi bhiṣak guhyed asaṃśayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.9">
                        <label>4.8.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmān na vivṛtaḥ kāryo vraṇas tu śataponake ||
                        <caesura/>
                         vyādhau tanu bahucchidre bhiṣajā sādhu jānatā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.10">
                        <label>4.8.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         arddhalāṅgalalakaś chedaḥ kāryo lāṅgalako 'pi vā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvatobhadrako vāpi kāryo gotīrthako 'pi vā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.11">
                        <label>4.8.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvānā srāvamārggas tu pradahed bhiṣag agninā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sukumārasya bhīroś ca duḥkaraḥ śataponakaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.12">
                        <label>4.8.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra dhīraḥ pramāṇajñaḥ svedam āśu prayojayet ||
                        <caesura/>
                         svedadravyair yathoktais tu kṛsarāpāyasais tathā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.13">
                        <label>4.8.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         grāmyānūpodakair mmāṃsair llāvādyair vvāpi viṣkiraiḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         vṛkṣādanīmathair aṇḍam bitvādiñ ca gaṇan tathā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.14">
                        <label>4.8.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyaṃ sukṛtaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ kumbhe nidhāpayet ||
                        <caesura/>
                         nāḍīsvedena tenāsya tad vraṇaṃ svedayet tataḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.15">
                        <label>4.8.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tilānatasibījāni yavagodhūmakodravān ||
                        <caesura/>
                         lavaṇāmlakavarggaś ca sthālyām ādhāya sādhayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.16">
                        <label>4.8.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āturaṃ svedayet tatra tathā sidhyati kurvvataḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         svinnañ ca pāyayed enaṃ kuṣṭhañ ca lavaṇāni ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.17">
                        <label>4.8.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vacāhiṅgvajamodaś ca samabhāgāni sarppiṣā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         mārdvīkenāthavāmlena surāsauvīrakeṇa vā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.18">
                        <label>4.8.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tato madhukatailena tasya siñced vraṇam bhiṣak ||
                        <caesura/>
                         pratisārayed gudañ cāsya tailair vvātarujāpahaiḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.19">
                        <label>4.8.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhinānena viṇmūtraṃ svamārggam anupadyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         anye copadravās tīvrāḥ sidhyanty atra na saṃśayaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.20">
                        <label>4.8.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         taponake samākhyātam uṣṭragrīve kriyāṃ śṛṇu ||
                        <caesura/>
                         eṣyoṣṭragrīvam āsādya cchitvā kṣāran nipātayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.21">
                        <label>4.8.21</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.22">
                        <label>4.8.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bandhaṃ yathāvat kurvvīta pariṣekaś ca sarppiṣā ||
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.23ab">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.23a">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.23cd">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.24">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.25">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.26">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.27">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.28">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.30">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.31">

                        <caesura/>
                         āgantuje bhiṣa<unclear extent="1" unit="char"/>ḍīṃ śastreṇotkṛtya yatnataḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.32">
                        <label>4.8.32</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.33">
                        <label>4.8.33</label>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.34">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.35">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.36">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.37">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.38">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.39">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.40">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.41">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.42">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.43">
                        <label>4.8.43</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rajanī triphalā tutthaṃ hitaṃ syād vraṇaśodhanam ||
                        <caesura/>
                         māgadhyo madhukaṃ lodhraṃ kuṣṭhamelā hareṇavaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.44">
                        <label>4.8.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samaṅgā dhātakī caiva sārivā rajanīdvayaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         priyaṅgavaḥ sarjjarasaṃ padmakam padmakesaraṃ | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.8.45">
                        <label>4.8.45</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mātuluṅgasya patrāṇi madhūcchiṣṭaṃ sasaindhavaṃ ||

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.9.1">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.9.4">
                        <label>4.9.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tvagdoṣī tu
                        mānsadugdhadadhitilakulatthamāṣaniṣpāvekṣuvikārāmlapiṣṭamayānividāhyābhiṣyandīni
                        divāsvapnavyavāyañ ca dūrata eva pariharet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.9.5">
                        <label>4.9.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ śāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmaśyāmākakoradūṣoddālakānanavām bhuñjīta |
                        mudgāḍhakyor anyatarasya sūpena yūṣeṇa vā || nambapattrāruṣkaraviyāmiśreṇa
                        maṇḍūkapaṇttyavalgujāṭarūṣakapuṣpaiḥ sarppiḥsiddhaiḥ sarṣapatailasiddhair vvā
                        | tiktavarggeṇa vābhihitena māṃsasātmyāya vā jāṅgalamānsasamedaṣkam vitaret
                        | tailam vajrakam abhyaṅgārthe āragvadhādikaṣāyamutsādanārthe |
                        pānapariṣekāvagāheṣu khadirakaṣāyam ity eṣa cāhāravibhāgaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.9.6">
                        <label>4.9.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra pūrvvarūpeṣūbhayataḥ | saṃśodhanam āseveta | tvakprāpte
                        saṃśodhanālepanāni | śoṇitaprāpte
                        saṃśodhanālepanakaṣāyapā|naśoṇitāvasecanāni | māṃsaprāpte
                        saṃśodhanālepanakaṣāyapānaśoṇitāvasekāriṣṭamanthaprāsān | caturthe
                        dhātuprāpte yāpyenātmavataḥ samvidhānavataś ca | tatra saṃśodhanāc
                        choṇitāvasekāc corddhvam bhallātaka<pc> </pc>śilāja<pc
                            > </pc>tukuruvaka<pc> </pc>khadirāsanāyaskṛtividhānam upaseveta |
                        pañcame naivopakramet </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.9.7">
                        <label>4.9.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra prathamam eva kuṣṭhinaṃ snehapānenopakramet |
                        meṣaśṛṅgīśvadaṃṣṭrāsāṅgaṣṭāguḍūcīdvipañcamūlasiddhantailaṃ ghṛtam vā
                        vātakuṣṭhinām pānābhyaṅgayor vvidadhyāt |
                        dhavāśvakarṇṇakakubhapalāśapicumarddamadhukalodhrasamaṅgāsiddhaṃ
                        pittakuṣṭhināṃ |
                        priyālasanāragvadhanimbasaptaparṇṇacitrakamaricavacākuṣṭhasiddhaṃ
                        śleṣmakuṣṭhināṃ | bhallātakaviḍaṅgasiddham vā sarvveṣāṃ
                        harītavyāmalakavibhītakapavolapicumarddāṭarūṣakakaṭurohiṇībhāradrāduṃrālabhātrāyamāṇāparppaṭakañcetyetad
                        dvipalikyānijalāḍhake prakṣipya tatkaṣāyam pādāvaśiṣṭam avatārya
                        ghṛtaprastham āvapet kalkapeṣyāṇi cemāni bheṣajāny arddhapalikyāni |
                        trāyamāṇāmustendrayavācandanakirātatiktakapippalyaś cety etat
                        mṛdvagnisiddham avatārya pāyayed etat tiktakan nāma sarppiḥ
                        kuṣṭhajvaragulmārśograhaṇīdoṣapāṇḍurogavisarppaṣāṇḍhyaśamanaś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.9.8">
                        <label>4.9.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saptaparṇṇātiviṣāśamyākakaṭurohiṇyamṛṇālaharītakyāmalakavibhītakapaṭolapicumarddaparppaṭakirātatiktakaharidrādurālabhātrāyamāṇāmustācandanapadmakaharidropakulyāviśvāmūrvvāśatāvarīśārivāṭarūṣakakuṭajendravāruṇīpātḥavṛkṣādanīgranthikā
                        ceti | samabhāgāni kalkaḥ syāc caturgguṇaṃ sarppiḥ prakṣipya tad dviguṇam
                        āmakaṃlarasas tac caturgguṇam āpas tad aikadhyaṃ mṛdvagnisiddham avatārya
                        pāyayed etan mahātiktakaṃ nāma sarppiḥ

                        ca śamayed ity </l>

                        madhumadhuram āmalakarasena |
                        kuṭajakapittharohītakavibhītakasaptaparṇṇapuṣyakalkam vā |

                        vyākhyātāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.11.9">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.11.11">
                        <label>4.11.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mahādhanamahitācāram auṣadhadveṣiṇam īśvaram vā pāṭhābhayācitrakapragāḍham
                        analpamākṣikam anyatamam āsavaṃ pāyayet | aṃgārakaśūlyopadaṃśam vā |
                        mārdvīntam abhīkṣṇam madhukapitthamaricānusiddhāni pānakāni cāsmai upaharet
                        | uṣṭrāśvatarapurīṣacūrṇṇāni cāsmai dadyād aśaneṣu || hiṅgusiddhaiś ca
                        yūṣaiḥ sārṣapaiś ca rāgai bhojayet | aviruddhāni cāsmai pānabhojanāny
                        upaharet | rasagandhavanti ca | pravṛddhamedas tu vyāyāmaniyuddha
                        krīḍāpahāya gajarathapādacaryāparikramaṇānyas trāpāstram vā seveta |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.11.12">
                        <label>4.11.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         adhanas tv avāndhavo vā pādatracchattrarahito bhaikṣāśīgrām aikarātravāsī
                        munir iva saṃyatātmā yo janaśatam adhikaṃ gacchet | mahādhano vā
                        śyāmākanīvārāmalakatindukakapitthāsmantakaphalamūlāhāro mṛgais saha vaset
                        mūtraśakṛdbhakṣaḥ | satatam anuvrajed vāgāḥ | vrāhmaṇo vā śiloñchavṛttir
                        bbhūtvā brahmaratham uddharet | kṛsetkṛśodatsa 2 satatasamitaṃ khaned vā
                        kūpaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.11.13">
                        <label>4.11.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātr || adhano vaidyasandeśā devaṃ kurvvaṇatandritaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samvatsarāntarāt puṃsaḥ pramehān pratimucyate iti || pra ||</l>

                        bhavati | tasyobhayataḥ saṃśodhanam evem akurvvataḥ | tasya doṣāḥ pravṛddhā
                        māṃsaśoṇitaṃ pradūṣya śophañ janayanti | upadravām̐ś kām̐ścit tatroktaḥ
                        pratīkāraḥ sirāmokṣaś ca | evam akurvvato vā tasya śophaḥ pravṛddho
                        'timātraṃ tad vidāham āpadyate | tatra śastrapraṇidhānam vraṇakriyopasevā ca

                <div n="14" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 14 (draft based on MS H)</head>



                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.1">
                        <label>4.14.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāta udarāṇāñ cikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.3">
                        <label>4.14.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aṣṭāv udarāṇi pūrvvam uktāṇi
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣv asādhyam baddhagudaṃ pariśrāvi ca | avaśiṣṭāni kṛcchrasādhyāni
                        sarvvāṇy eva pratyākhyāyopakrameta | teṣv ādyaś caturvvarggo bheṣajasādhyaḥ
                        | uttaraḥ śastrasādhyaḥ | kālaprakarṣāt sarvvāṇy eva śastrasādhyāni bhavanti
                        | varjjayitavyāni vā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.4">
                        <label>4.14.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         udarī tu gurvabhiṣyandirūkṣavidāhyatisnigdhapiśitapariṣekāvagāhān pariharet
                        | śāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmanīvārān nityam aśnīyāt | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.5">
                        <label>4.14.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vātodariṇam vidārigandhādisiddhena sarppiṣā snehayitvā,
                        tilvakavipakvenānulomya citrāphalatailapragāḍhena
                        vidārigandhādikaṣāyeṇāsthāpayed anuvāsayec ca | sālvaṇenopanāhayed udaraṃ |
                        bhojayec cainam vidārigandhādisiddhena payasā jāṅgalarasena vā | svedayec
                        cābhīkṣṇam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.6">
                        <label>4.14.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pittodariṇaṃ tu madhuragaṇavipakvena sarppiṣā snehayitvā
                        śyāmātrivṛttriphalāvipakvenānulomya śarkkarāmadhughṛtapragāḍhena
                        nyagrodhādikaṣāyeṇāsthāpayed anuvāsayec ca | pāyasenopanāhayed udaraṃ |
                        bhojayec cainaṃ vidārigandhādisiddhena kṣīreṇa || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.7">
                        <label>4.14.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śleṣmodariṇan tu pippalyādisiddhena sarppiṣā snehayitvā snuhākṣīravipakvena
                        cānulomya trikaṭukamūtratailapragāḍhena muṣkakādikvāthenāsthāpayed
                        anuvāsayec ca | kīkiṇvasarṣapamūlakabījaiś copanāhayed udaraṃ | bhojayec
                        cainan trikaṭukapragāḍhena kulatthayūṣeṇa | pāyasena vā | svedayec
                        cābhīkṣṇaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.8">
                        <label>4.14.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dūṣyodariṇaṃ tu saptalāśaṃkhinīsvarasasiddhena sarppiṣā virecayet | māsam
                        arddhamāsam vā mahāsnuhīvṛkṣakṣīragomūtrasiddhena vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.9">
                        <label>4.14.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gopitānilamūlatvāt sañcitatvāt malasya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvodareṣu saṃsanti bahuśas tv anulomanaṃ ||0|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.10">
                        <label>4.14.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrddhvan sāmānyānyogān vakṣyāmaḥ || eraṇḍatailam evāharahar mmāsam ekaṃ
                        dvau vā kevalaṃ mūtrayuktaṃ kṣīrayuktaṃ vā sevetodakavarjjī | mahiṣīmūtraṃ
                        kṣīreṇa nirāhāraḥ saptarātraṃ | uṣṭrīkṣīrāhāro vānnapānaparivārivarjjī
                        pakṣaṃ | pippalīr vvā māsaṃ pūrvvoktena vidhānena vāseveta |
                        saindhavājamodanimbasiddham vā nikumbhatailaṃ |
                        ārddrakaṣṭaṅgaṇakṣārapātrārddhasiddham vā | śatapuṣpasiddham vā vātaśūle
                        vacāryaṃ | śṛṅgaverarasavipakvam vā kṣīram āseveta | cavyāśṛṅgaverakalkam vā
                        payasā | saralāmaradārucittrakam eva vā |
                        muruṅgīśālaparṇṇīśyāmāpunarṇṇavājyotiṣkaphalātailam vā kṣīreṇa |
                        svarjjikāhiṃgumiśram pibet | guḍadvitīyo vā harītakīm bhakṣayet |
                        snuhākṣīrapariśrāvitānām vā pippalīnāṃ sahasraṅ kālena | pathyācūrṇṇam vā
                        snuhākṣīraparibhāvitamutkārikām vā paktvā dāpayet | harītakīcūrṇṇaprastham
                        āḍhake ghṛtasyāvāpya khajenābhimathyānuguptan nidhāyārddhamāsaṃ yavapalle
                        vāsayet | tataś coddhṛtya pariśrāvya mahatīharītakīkvāthāmladadhīnyāvāpya
                        vipaced yathāyogam māsam arddhamāsam vā pāyayet | gavye payasi
                        mahāvṛkṣakṣīram āvāpya vipacet || vipakvañ cāvatārya śītībhūtaṃ
                        manthānenābhimathya navanītam ādāya bhūyo mahāvṛkṣakṣīrakaṣāyeṇaiva saha
                        vipacet | tad yathāyogam māsam arddhamāsam vā pāyayet |
                        cavyacitrakadantyativiṣākuṣṭhaśārivāviḍaṃgatriphalājamodaharidrādāruharidrāśaṃkhinītṛvṛtkaṭukānām
                        arddhakārṣikā bhāgāḥ | rājavṛkṣaphalamajjo 'aṣṭau karṣāḥ |
                        mahāvṛkṣakṣīrapale dve | gavāṃ kṣīramūtrayor aṣṭāvaṣṭau palāni | tat sarvvaṃ
                        ghṛtaprasthe samāvāpya vipacet | tathāyogam māsam arddhamāsam vā pāyayet |
                        etāni khalu tilvakaghṛtacaturthāni sarppīṃṣy
                        udaragulmavidradhyaṣṭhīlānāhakuṣṭhonmādāpasmāreṣūpayojyāni | virecanārtham
                        mūtrāsavāriṣṭasurāś cābhīkṣṇam mahāvṛkṣakṣīrasambhṛtāḥ seveta |
                        virecanadravyakaṣāyam vā śṛṅgaveradevadārupragāḍhaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.11">
                        <label>4.14.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vamanavirecanadravyāṇām palikābhāgāḥ |
                        pippalyādivacādiharidrādiparipaṭhitānāñ ca dravyāṇāṃ ślakṣṇapiṣṭānāṃ
                        yathoktānāñ ca lavaṇānān tat sarvvam mūtragaṇe prakṣipya
                        mahāvṛkṣakṣīraprasthañ ca mṛdvagnināvaghaṭṭayan vipacet | avidagdhakalkan
                        tatsādhusiddham avatārya śītībhūtam aṅguṣṭhamātrāṅ guṭikām varttayet | tāsām
                        ekāṃ dve tisro vā yathāyogam māsām̐s trīṃś caturo vā seveta | eṣā khalu
                        mūtravarttikriyāviśeṣeṇa mahāvyādhiṣūpayujyate | koṣṭhajām̐ś ca krimīn
                        upahanti kāsaśvāsapratiśyāyārocakāvipākodāvarttām̐ś ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.12">
                        <label>4.14.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         madanaphalamajjājīmūtakekṣvākutrikaṭukasarṣapalavaṇāni mūtrakṣārayor
                        anyatareṇa piṣṭvāṅguṣṭhamātrāvarttī kṛtvodariṇaḥ | ānāhe tu
                        tailalavaṇagudābhyaktasyaikāṃ dve ca pāyau nidadhyāt | eṣānāhavarttikriyā
                        vātamūtrapurīṣodāvarttādhmānānāheṣu vidheyā | dūṣyodariṇan tu
                        vyoṣāśvamārakaguñjākākādanīmūlakalkam pāyayet | ikṣukāṇḍāni vā kṛṣṇasarpeṇa
                        daṃśayitvā bhakṣayet | vallīphalāni vā kandajam vā mūlajam vā viṣam āseveta
                        | tenāgadībhavaty anyataram vā bhāvam āpadyate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.13">
                        <label>4.14.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         plīhodariṇas tūpasnigdhasvinnasya dadhnā bhuktavato vāmabāhukurpparasandhāv
                        abhyantarasirām vidhyet | vimarddayec ca pāṇinā plīhānaṃ |
                        rudhiraprasyandanārthan tataḥ śuddhadehaṃ samudraśuktikṣāram payasā pāyayeta
                        | hiṅgusauvarccikām vā kṣīreṇa | śrutena vā palāśakṣāreṇa |
                        yavakṣārapārijātakekṣurakāpāmārggakṣāram vā tailasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ |
                        saubhāñjanakayūṣaṃ vā pippalīsaindhavacitrakayuktam amlapūtikarañjakṣāram vā
                        | viḍaṅgalavaṇapippalīprāgāḍhaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.14">
                        <label>4.14.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pippalīpippalīmūlaṃ śṛṅgaveracitrakayavakṣārasaindhavānām palikā bhāgāḥ |
                        ghṛtaprasthaṃ tattulyaṃ kṣīran tadekadhyam vipācayed etat khalu ṣaṭpalakaṃ
                        plīhāgnisādagulmodāvarttaśvayathupāṇḍurogaśvāsakāsapratiśyāyor
                        ddhvavātaviṣamajvarān upahanti ||
                        pipplalīmaricaśṛṅgaverahiṅgusaindhavasauvarccalaviḍadāḍimayavānikāpuṣkaramūlājājīdhānyāmlavetasakṣāradvayavacācittrakailājagandhātulasītyetaiḥ
                        samair ghṛtaprasthan dadhi caturgguṇaṃ bījapūrakarasayuktam pācayed etad
                        dādhikaṃ sarppir ddīpanīyam
                        udaragulmakāsaśvāsajvaravidradyaṣṭhīlānāhasarvvavātarukchamanaṃ śūlaghnañ
                        ceti || śṛṅgaveramātuluṅgarasadāḍimadadhiśuṣkamūlakolāmlakaṣāyaprastheṣu
                        ghṛtaprasthañ cāvāpya | pañca kolaviḍaṅgayavānīśuṣkamūlapāṭhagarbbhan tan
                        siddham pāyayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.15">
                        <label>4.14.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yakṛddālye 'py eṣa eva kriyāvibhāgaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣatas tu dakṣiṇabāhau sirām vidhyet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.16">
                        <label>4.14.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         maṇibandhe samunnāmya vāmam aṅguṣṭham īritaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dahet sirāṃ śareṇāśu plīho vaidyaḥ praśāntaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.17">
                        <label>4.14.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         baddhagude parisrāvini ca snigdhasvinnasyādho nābher vvāmataś caturaṅgulam
                        apahāya romarājyād udaraṃ pāṭayitvā caturaṅgulapramāṇamantrāṇi niṣkṛṣya
                        nirīkṣya baddhagudasyāntrapratirodhakaramasmānaṃ bālam vāpohya malajātan
                        tato madhu sarppiṣābhyajyāntrāṇi yathāsthānaṃ sthāpayitvā bāhyaṃ vraṇam
                        udarasya sīvyet | parisrāviṇo py evam antraṃ samānayitvā cchidraṃ
                        kālapipīlikābhir ddaṅśayet | daṣṭe ca tāsāṃ kāyān upaharec chinnaśirāṃsi
                        tataḥ pūrvvavat sīvyet | vāsayec cainan tailadroṇyām alpam vā payovṛttir iti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.18">
                        <label>4.14.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         udakodariṇas tu tailābhyaktasyoṣṇodakaparisvinnasyāptaiḥ
                        suparigṛhītasyākakṣāt paṭūveṣṭitasyārdho nābheś caturaṅgulam apahāya
                        romarāmāṇyardvyaṅgulam vrīhimukhenāṅguṣṭhodaramātram vidārya trapvādīnām
                        anyatamasya nāḍīm ubhayato dvāraṃ saṃyojya doṣodakam avasiñcen na caikasmin
                        divase sarvvadoṣodakam apaharet || sahasāpahyate doṣe
                        tṛṣṇājvarāṅgamarddātīsāraśvāsakāsapādadāhā utpadyeran | āpūryate vā
                        dṛḍhataram asañjātaprāṇasya tasmāt tṛtīyañ caturtham pañcamaṃ ṣaṣṭham
                        aṣṭamam vā dvādaśam vā divasam antaraṃ doṣodakam alpam alpam avasiñcet |
                        nisrute nisrute doṣe gāḍhataram āvikakauṣeyacarmmaṇām anyatamena
                        pariveṣṭayed udaran tathā nādhmāpayati vāyuḥ ṣaṇmāsām̐ś ca bhojayet payasā
                        rasena vā | tatas trīn māsānavodakena phalāmlena vāvaśiṣṭam māsatrayam annaṃ
                        laghu hitaṃ seveta evaṃ samvatsareṇāgadībhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.14.19">
                        <label>4.14.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra||
                        <caesura/>
                         āsthāpane caiva virecane ca pāne tathāhāravidhikriyāsu |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvodarāṇāṃ kuśalena yojyaṃ kṣīraṃ raso jāṅgalajo tha vā syād iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.1">
                        <label>4.15.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto mūḍhagarbhbhacikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.3">
                        <label>4.15.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nātaḥ kaṣṭataramasti yathā mūḍhagarbhbhoddharaṇamatra hi
                        yoniyakṛtplīhāntragarbhbhāśayānām madhye kartavyaṃ | sparśeno
                        tkarṣāyakarṣaṇāpakarttanabhedanavyāvarttanapīḍanārjjūkaraṇāni caikahastena
                        garbhbhamahiṃsatā garbhbhiṇīñ cāhiṃsatā tasmād adhikṛtya tam āpṛcchya parañ
                        ca yan namāsthāyopakrameta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.4">
                        <label>4.15.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra samāsenāṣṭavidha mūḍhagarbhbhagatiruddiṣṭā svabhāvagatā vapi tu
                        trayaḥ saṅgā bhavanti śiraso vaipulyādaṃśayor jjaghanasya vā </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.5">
                        <label>4.15.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jīvati garbhbhe sūtyaḥ prayateran |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirharaṇe cyāvanāṃś ca mantrānanuśrāvayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.6">
                        <label>4.15.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ihāmṛtaś ca somaś ca citrabhānuś ca bhāvini |
                        <caesura/>
                         uccaiḥśravāś ca turago mandire nivasantu te || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.7">
                        <label>4.15.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         idamamṛtamapāṃ samuddhṛtāṃ vai tava laghu garbhbhamimam pramuñcahe stri |
                        <caesura/>
                         tad analapavanārkkavāsavās te saha lavaṇāmbudharair ddiśantu śāntiṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.8"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.9">
                        <label>4.15.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         oṣadhāni ca vidadhyād yathoktāni ca | mṛte cottānāyā bhugnasakthinyā
                        vastracumbhalakonnāmitakaṭyā dhanvakamṛttikāśālmalīmṛtsnaghṛtābhyām
                        mrakṣayitvā hastaṃ yonyām praveśya garbhbham apaharet tatra śakthibhyām
                        āgatam anulomam evāñchet | ekasakthi pratipannasyetaraṃ sakthi prasārya
                        sphigdeśāgataṃ sphigdeśaṃ prapīḍyorddhvam utkṣipya sakthinī
                        prasāryasyāpaharet | tiryag āgatasya parighasyeva tiryak cīnasya paścād
                        arddhamūrddham utkṣipya pūrvvārddham apatyapathaṃ
                        pratyārjjavamānayitvāpaharet | dvāvanty āvasādhyau mūḍhagarbhbhau bhavataḥ |
                        evam aśakye śastram avatārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.10">
                        <label>4.15.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sacetanan tu śastreṇa na kathañcana dārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         ātmānañ jananīñ caiva hanyād āśu sacetanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.11"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.12">
                        <label>4.15.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ striyam āśvāsya maṇḍalāgreṇāṅguliśastreṇa vā śiro vidārya
                        śiraḥkapālāny āhṛtya śaṃkunā saṃgṛhyor asi kakṣe cāpaharet | abhinnaśiram
                        vākṣikūṭo gaṇḍe vā asaṃsaktasyāṃśadeśe bāhūṃ cchhitvā dṛtim ivātatam
                        vātapūrṇṇodaram vidārya nirasyātrāṇi śithilībhūtāṃ | jaghanaśaktasya vā
                        jaghanakapālānīti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.13">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.32">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.33">
                        <label>4.15.33</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         tat sādhusiddhaṃ sauvarṇṇe rājate mṛnmaye 'pi vā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.34">
                        <label>4.15.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣipya kalase 'bhyarccya svanuguptan nidhāpayet ||
                        <caesura/>
                         balātailamidan nāmnā sarvvavātavikāranut | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.35">
                        <label>4.15.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathābalam ato mātrāṃ sūtikāyai pradāpayet ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yā ca garbhbhārthinī nārī kṣīṇaśukraś ca yaḥ pumān | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.36">
                        <label>4.15.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātakṣīṇe marmmahate mathite 'bhihate tathā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         bhagne sramābhipanne ca sarvvathaiva prayujyate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.37">
                        <label>4.15.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvān āpekṣakādīṃś ca vātavyādhīn apohati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         hikkāśvāsam adhīmanthaṅ gulmaṅ kāsañ ca dustaraṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.38">
                        <label>4.15.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaṇmāsān upayujyena mantravṛddhir vvyapohati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         pratyagradhātuḥ puruṣo bhavec ca sthirayauvanaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.39">
                        <label>4.15.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         etad dhirājñāṅ karttavyaṃ rājāmātyāś ca ye narāḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhinaḥ sukumārāś ca dhaninaś cāpi ye narāḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.40">
                        <label>4.15.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         balākaṣāyapītebhyas tilebhyo vā py anekaśaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tailam utpādya tat tailaṃ śatapākakṛtaṃ śubhaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.41">
                        <label>4.15.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śaste 'hni nibhṛtaveśmany upayuñjyād yathābalaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         jīrṇṇesmin payasā siddhaṃ ṣaṣṭikānnam avāpnuyāt | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.42">
                        <label>4.15.42</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         anena vidhinā droṇam upayuñjyānnamīritaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         bhuñjīta dviguṇaṃ kālaṃ balavarṇṇānvitas tataḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.43">
                        <label>4.15.43</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvapāpair vvinirmmuktaḥ śatāyuḥ puruṣo bhavet ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śataṃ śataṃ cotkarṣād droṇe droṇe prakīrttyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.44">
                        <label>4.15.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         balākalpenātibalāguḍūcyādity avalliṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         śairīyake vīratare śatāvaryān trikaṇṭake || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.45">
                        <label>4.15.45</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailāni kuryāt madhukaprasāraṇyoś ca buddhimān | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.46"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.15.47">
                        <label>4.15.47</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvveṣām eva caiteṣām upayogañ cikitsakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         balātailavadācaṣṭe guṇāṃś caivā viśeṣata iti ||</l>







                </div>

                <div n="16" type="adhyāya">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.1">
                        <label>4.16.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto vidradhīnāñ cikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="Su.4.16.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.3">
                        <label>4.16.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         uktā vidradhayo ye ṣaṭ teṣv asādhyas tu sarvvajaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śeṣeṣv āmeṣu karttavyā tvaratā śophavat kriyā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.4">
                        <label>4.16.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātaghnamūlakalkais tu vasātailaghṛtāyutaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhoṣṇo vahalo lepaḥ prayojyo vātavidradhau ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.5">
                        <label>4.16.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sānūpaudakamānsas tu kākolyādiś ca yogaṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehāmlasiddho lavaṇaḥ prayojyaś copanāhane ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.6">
                        <label>4.16.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         veśavāraiḥ sakṛsaraiḥ payobhiḥ pāyasais tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedayec cāpi satatam āharec cāpi śoṇitaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.7">
                        <label>4.16.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sa ced evam upakrāntaḥ pākāya vimukho yadi |
                        <caesura/>
                         tam pācayitvā śastreṇa bhidyād bhitvā ca buddhimān ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.8">pañcamūlīkaṣāyeṇa prakṣālya lavaṇottaraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tilair bbhadrādimadhukasaṃyutaiḥ pūrya veṣṭayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.9">vairecanikayuktena trivṛtena viśodhya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pṛthakparṇṇyādisiddhena trivṛte naiva ropayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.10">paittikaṃ śarkkarālājamadhukaiḥ śārivāyutaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pradihyāt kṣīrapiṣṭair vvā payasyośīracandanaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.11">pākyaiḥ śītakaṣāyair vvā kṣīrair ikṣurasais tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         jīvanīyaghṛtair vvāpi secayec charkkarāyutaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.12">tṛvṛddharītakīnāñ ca cūrṇṇam madhuyutaṃ lihet |
                        <caesura/>
                         jalaukābhir hareccāsṛk pakvam vāpāṭya buddhimān ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.13">kṣīravṛkṣakaṣāyeṇa prakṣālyodakajena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tilaiḥ sayaṣṭīmadhukaiḥ sāmṛtaiḥ sarppiṣāyutaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.14">pratigrāhya pratanunā sarppiṣāveṣṭayed vraṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prapauṇḍarīkamañjiṣṭhā madhukośīrapadmakaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.15">saharidraiḥ kṛtaṃ sarppiḥ sakṣīraṃ vraṇaropaṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīraśuklāpṛthakparṇṇīsamaṅgālodhracandanaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.16">nyagrodhādipravāleṣu teṣāṃ tvakṣvathavākṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         naktamālasya patrāṇi paṭolāriṣṭayos tathā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.17"> dve haridre madhūcchiṣṭaṃ madhukan tiktarohiṇī |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.18">priyaṃgukuśamūlañ ca niculasya tvageva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.19">eṣāṃ karṣasamair bbhāgair ghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         duṣṭavraṇapraśamanaṃ tathā nāḍīvināśanaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.20">sadyaś cchinnavraṇānāñ ca karañjādyamidaṃ śubhaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.21"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.22">iṣṭakāsikatālohagośakṛttuṣapāṅśubhiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.23">mūtrair uṣṇaiś ca satataṃ svedayec chleṣmavidradhiṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyapānair vvamanair ālepair upanāhanaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.24">hared doṣān abhīkṣṇañ ca tathaivāsṛg alāvubhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āragvadhakaṣāyeṇa pakvam vā pāṭya dhāvayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.25">haridrātriphalāśaktutilair mmadhusamāyutaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrayitvā vraṇaṃ samyak vadhnīyāt kīrttitaṃ yathā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.26">tataḥ kulatthikādantī tṛvṛcchyāmārkkatilvakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryāt tailaṃ sagomūtraṃ hitan tatra sasaindhavaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.27">pittavidradhivat sarvvā kriyā niravaśeṣataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidradhyoḥ kuśalaḥ kuryād raktāgantunimittayoḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.28">varuṇādir gaṇakvātham apakve 'bhyantarotthite |
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣakādipratīvāpaṃ pivecchaṃkaraṇā yadi ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.29">anayor vvarggayoḥ sarppiḥ siddhaṃ vairecaneṣu ca ||
                        <caesura/>
                         vidradhiṃ hanti na cirāt prātaḥ prātar nniṣevitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.30">ebhir eva gaṇaiś cāpi saṃsiddhaṃ snehayojitaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kāryam āsthāpanaṃ kṣipraṃ sa ca sneho nuvāsanaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.31">pānālepana bhojyeṣu madhusigrudrumo 'pi vā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         dattāvāyo yathādoṣam apakvaṃ hanti vidradhiṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.32">toyadhānyānyāmlamūtrais tu peyo vāpi surādibhiḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yathādoṣagaṇakvāthaiḥ pived vāpi śilājatuṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.33">pradhānaṅ guggulum vāpi dāruśuṇṭhīm athāpi vā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         svedopanāhaḥ kuryāc ca sadā cāpy anulomayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.34">śirāṃ yathoktām vidhyeta kaphaje vidradhau bhiṣak ||
                        <caesura/>
                         raktapittānilottheṣu kecid vāhau vadanti tu |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.35">paryāgatañ ca śastreṇa bhittvā vraṇavad ācaret ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śruteṣūrddham adho vāpi maireyāmlasurāsavaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.36">peyo varuṇakādis tu madhusigrudrumo 'pi vā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         madhusigros tu mūleṣu siddhānāṃ sahasāvudhaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.37">yavakolakulatthānāṃ yūṣair bbhuñjīta mānavaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         prātaḥ prātaś ca seveta mātrayā tailvakaṃ ghṛtaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.38"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.16.39">paryāgate vidradho tu siddhir nnaikāntikī bhaved iti || </l>

                <div n="17" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 17 (draft based on MS H)</head>



                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.1">
                        <label>4.17.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto visarppanāḍīstanarogāṇāñ cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.3">
                        <label>4.17.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhyā visarppās traya ādito ye tat sannipātakṣatajāvasādhyau |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhyeṣu pathyair hi gaṇair vvidadhyād ghṛtāvasekoś ca tathā pradehān
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.4">
                        <label>4.17.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kuṣṭhaṃ śatāhvāsuradārumustāvārāhikustuṃvurukṛṣṇagandhā |
                        <caesura/>
                         vāterkkavaṃśārttagaṇās tu yojyā sekeṣu lepeṣu tathā ghṛteṣu ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.5">
                        <label>4.17.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yat pañcamūlaṃ khalu kaṇṭakākhyam alpam mahac cāpy athavallijāñ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         taccopayojyam bhiṣajā pradehaiḥ seke ghṛte cāpi tathaiva taile ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.6">
                        <label>4.17.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaseruśṛṅgāṭakapadmagundrāḥ saśaivalāḥ sotpalakarddamām̐ś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vastrāntarā pittakṛte visarppalepāvidheyāḥ saghṛtāḥ suśītāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.7">
                        <label>4.17.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hrīveralāmajjakacandanāni śrotojamuktāmaṇigairikaiś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīrābhipiṣṭāḥ saghṛtāḥ suśītā lepāḥ prayojyās tanavaḥ sukhāya ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.8">
                        <label>4.17.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mañjīṣṭhayaṣṭīmadhukam payasyāprapauṇḍarīkaṃ saha padmakena |
                        <caesura/>
                         saugandhikāñ ceti sukhapralepaḥ paitte visarppe bhiṣajā prayojyāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.9">
                        <label>4.17.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nyagrodhavarggam pariṣecanañ ca ghṛtañ ca kuryāt svarasena tasya |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītaiḥ payo bhiś ca madhūdakaiś ca saśarkkarair ikṣurasaiś ca sekāṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.10">
                        <label>4.17.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ghṛtañ ca gaurīmadhukāravindalodhrāmvurājādanajīvakeṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathārṣabhe padmakaśārivāyāṃ kākoli2medākumudotpaleṣu ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.11">
                        <label>4.17.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sacandanāyām madhuśarkkarāyān drākṣāsthirāpṛṣṇisamaṅgayā ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkīkṛtāsūdakamatragandhā nyagrodhavarggasya ca śārivādeḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.12">
                        <label>4.17.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gaṇasya vilvādikapañcamūlyoś caturgguṇaṃ kṣīramathāpi tadvat |
                        <caesura/>
                         prasthaṃ vipakvaṃ pariṣecanena paittāni hanyāt tu visapppanāḍī ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.13">
                        <label>4.17.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         visphoṭaduṣṭavraṇaśīrṣarogān pākan tathāsyāsya tathaiva pānāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         grahārddite śoṣiṇi cāpi vāle | ghṛtaṃ tu gaurādikam etad iṣṭaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.14">
                        <label>4.17.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāśvagandhā saralātha kālā saikeṣikāvāpyathavājaśṛṅgī |
                        <caesura/>
                         gomūtrapiṣṭo vihimapradeho hanyādvisarppaṅkaphajaṃ suśīghraṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.15">kālānusāryāgurucocaguñjārasnāvacāśītaśivendraparṇṇyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pālindimajjāsamahīkadam vā hito visarppeṣu kaphātmakeṣu ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.16">
                        <label>4.17.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gaṇas tu sarvvo varuṇaḥ prayojyaḥ kriyāsu sarvvāsu vicakṣaṇena |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvveṣu saṃśodhanam eva kuryād raktāvasekañ ca jalāyukābhiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.17">
                        <label>4.17.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvām̐ś ca pakvān pariśodhya dhīmān vraṇaṃ krameṇopacared yathoktaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāḍītridoṣaprabhavā na sidhye ccheṣāś catasraḥ khalu yatnasādhyāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.18">
                        <label>4.17.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrānilotthām upanāhya pūrvvam aśeṣataḥ pūyagatim vidārya |
                        <caesura/>
                         phalair apāmārggabhavaiḥ supiṣṭaiḥ sasaindhavaiḥ pūrya hitāya vadhyet
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.19">
                        <label>4.17.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣālane cāpi sadā vraṇasya yojyam mahad yat khalu pañcamūlaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hiṃsrā haridre kaṭukāvale ca gojihvikā caiva savilvamūlaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.20">
                        <label>4.17.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sambhṛtya kuryāt trivṛtaṃ vraṇasya saṃśodhanaṃ śodhanaropaṇajñaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittātmakāṃn prāg upanāhya dhīmān utkārikābhiḥ sapayoghṛtābhiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.21">
                        <label>4.17.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nipātyaśastran tilanāgadantīmañjiṣṭhakalkaiḥ pratipūrayīta |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣālane cāpi haridrasomanimvāḥprayojyāḥ kuśalena nityaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.22">
                        <label>4.17.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śyāmātribhaṇḍītriphalāsu siddhaṃ haridrayos tilvakavṛkṣake ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         ghṛtaṃ sadugdham vraṇatarppaṇena hanyād gatiṃ koṣṭhagatāpi yā syāt ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.23">
                        <label>4.17.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nāḍīṅ kaphotthām upanāhayitvā kulatthasiddhārthakaśaktukiṇvaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mṛdvīkṛtāmeṣyagatim viditvā nipātayec chastram aśeṣakārī ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.24">
                        <label>4.17.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dadyād vraṇe nimvatilāṃ sadantīṃ surāṣṭrajāṃ saindhavasamprayuktāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣālane cāpi karañjanimvajātyakṣapīlusvarasāḥ prayojyāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.25">
                        <label>4.17.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         suvarccikāsaindhavacitrakeṣu nikumbhanīlīta larūpikāsu |
                        <caesura/>
                         phaleṣv apāmārggabhaveṣu caiva kuryāt samamūtreṣu hitāya tailaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.26">
                        <label>4.17.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nāḍīn tu śalyaprabhavāṃ vidārya nirghātyaśalyaṃ pravidārya mārggaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vandhed vraṇaṃ kṣaudraghṛtapragāḍhaṃ datvā tilāñ cchodhyavaropayīta ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.27">
                        <label>4.17.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kumbhīkakharjjūrakapitthavilvavanaspatīnāñ ca śalāṭuvargge |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛtvā kaṣāyam vipacet tu tailam āvāpya mustāśakunapriyaṅgūḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.28">
                        <label>4.17.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saugandhikāmocarasāhipuṣpaṃ lodhrāṇi datvā khalu dhātakīñ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         etena śalyaprabhavā tu nāḍī rohed vraṇe vā sukhamāśu caiva ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.29">
                        <label>4.17.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛśadurvvalabhīrūṇān nāḍīm marmmāśritām api |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣārasūtreṇa tāṃ cchindyān na tu śastreṇa dārayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.30">
                        <label>4.17.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         eṣaṇyā gam anviṣya kṣārasūtrānuśāriṇīṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sūcīn nidadhyād gatyante pronnām pāṇḍu vinirharet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.31">
                        <label>4.17.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sūtrasyāntaṃ samānīya gāḍhavandhaṃ samācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ kṣāravalam vīkṣya sūtram anyat prayojayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.32">
                        <label>4.17.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣārāktam matimān vaidyo yāvanna cchidyate gatiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhagandare 'pyeṣa vidhiḥ kāryā vaidyena jānatā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.33">
                        <label>4.17.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         arvvudādiṣu cotkṣipya mūle sūtran nidhāpayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sūcībhir yavavaktrābhir ācitam vā samantataḥ |.
                        <caesura/>
                         mūle sūtre ca vadhnīyāc cchinne copakramed vraṇaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.34">
                        <label>4.17.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yā dvivraṇīye 'bhihitās tu varttyas tāḥ sarvvanāḍīṣu bhiṣag vidadhyāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         ghoṇṭāphalaṃ tvag madanaṃ phalañ ca pūgasya ca tvag lavaṇañ ca mukhyaṃ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.35">
                        <label>4.17.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snuhārkkadugdhena sahaiṣa kalko varttīkṛtā hantya cireṇa nāḍīṃ >
                        <caesura/>
                         vibhītakāmrāsthivaṭapravālahareṇukāśaṃkhinivījamisrā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.36">
                        <label>4.17.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         varāhaviṭsūkṣmamasīpradeyā nāḍīṣu tailena vimiśrayitvā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.38">
                        <label>4.17.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā ca gomāṃsamasīṃ hitāya koṣṭhāśritā svādarato diśanti |.
                        <caesura/>
                         varttīkṛtam mākṣikasaṃprayuktan nāḍīghnamuktaṃ lavaṇottamam vā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.39">
                        <label>4.17.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         duṣṭavraṇe yad vihitaṃ ca tailan tat sevyamānaṅ gatim āśu hanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.37">
                        <label>4.17.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhattūrakam madanakodravajañ ca vījaṃ kośātakī śukanasā mṛgabhojinī ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sāṅkollavījakusumais tu kṛtañ ca cūrṇṇaṃ lākṣodakāhṛtamalāsu gatīṣu deyaṃ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.40">
                        <label>4.17.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         eṣv eva sādhuṣu kṛteṣu vimiśrayitvā tailaṃ kṛtaṅ gatim apohati saptarātrāt
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṇḍīkṛtasya tu varāhavibhāvitasya mūleṣu kandaśakaleṣu ca sauvaheṣu ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.41">
                        <label>4.17.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṅ kṛtaṅ gatim apohati śīghram eva kandeṣu cāmaravarāyudhasāhvayeṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhallātakārkkamaricair llavaṇottamena siddhaṃ viḍaṃgarajanīdvayacitrakair
                        yat ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.42">
                        <label>4.17.42</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         syāmārkkavasya ca rasena nihanti tailaṃ nāḍīṃ kaphānilakṛtānapacīn vraṇām̐ś
                        ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         stanye gate vikṛtim āśu bhiṣak tu dhātrīṃ pītvā ghṛtaṃ pariṇatehani
                        vāmayīta ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.43">
                        <label>4.17.43</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nimvodakena madhumāgadhikāyutena vāntāpare 'hani ca mudgarasāsanā syāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         evan tryahañ caturahaṃ ṣaḍaham vamed vā sarppiḥ pived triphalayā saha
                        saṃyutam vā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.44">
                        <label>4.17.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhārggīm vacām ativiṣāṃ suradārupāṭhām mustādikam madhurasāṅ kaṭurohiṇīñ ca
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhātrī pivet tu payasaḥ pariśodhanārtha mustāvacādi tu varam madhunātha
                        vāpi ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.45">
                        <label>4.17.45</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         stanarogam utthitam avekṣya bhiṣag vidadhyād yad vidradhāvabhihitam
                        bahudhābhidhānam ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.46"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.17.47">
                        <label>4.17.47</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āme vidahyati tathaiva gate ca pākan tasyā stanau satatam eva ca
                        nirdduhīteti ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer">.. cikitsā <unclear extent="2" unit="syllables"/>.. o ||</p>

                <div corresp="4.18 in NAK 5-333" n="18" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 18 (draft based on MS H)</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.1">
                        <label>4.18.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto granthyapacyarbbudagalagaṇḍānāñ cikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.3">
                        <label>4.18.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         granthiṣv athāmeṣu bhiṣag vidadhyāc chophakriyā vistaraśo vidhijñaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.3a">
                        <label>4.18.3a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣed balañ cāpi narasya nityaṃ tad rakṣitam vyādhibalan nihanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.4">
                        <label>4.18.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ pibet sarppiratha dvayaṃ vā datvā vasām vā trivṛtam vidadhyāt|
                        apīhavātedaśamūlasiddhaṃ vaidyaścatuḥsnehamathāpi dadyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.5">
                        <label>4.18.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hiṃsrāsa rohiṇyamṛtātha bharggī śyonākabilvāgurukṛṣṇagandhā | gojī ca piṣṭā
                        saha tālapattryā granthau vidheyā nilaje pralepaḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.6">
                        <label>4.18.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svedopanāhā vividhāś ca yojyāḥ kuryāt prasiddhānaparāṃś ca lepān| vidārya
                        pakvaṃ samupohya pūyam prakṣālya bilvārkkagaṇaditoyaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.7">
                        <label>4.18.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tilaiḥ sapañcāṅgulapattramiśraiḥ saṃśodhayet saindhavasaṃprayuktaiḥ|
                        śuddham vraṇañ cāpy uparopayīta tailena rāsnāsaralāyutena|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.8">
                        <label>4.18.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viḍaṅgayaṣṭīmadhukāmṛtābhiḥ siddhena taṃ kṣīravimiśritena| jalāyukāḥ
                        pittakṛte hitās tu kṣīrodakābhyām pariṣecanañ ca|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.9">
                        <label>4.18.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kākolivarggasya tu śītalāni pibet kaṣāyāṇi saśarkkarāṇi |
                        drākṣārasenekṣurasena vāpi cūrṇṇaṃ pibed vāpi harītakīnāṃ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.10">
                        <label>4.18.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         madhūkajambvarjjunavetasānāṃ tvagbhiḥ pradehān avacārayec ca| saśarkkarair
                        vvā tṛṇaśūlyakandair ddihyād abhīkṣṇaṃ mucilindajair vvā|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.11">
                        <label>4.18.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vidārya vā pakvamapohya pūyaṃ dhāvet kaṣāyeṇa vanaspatīnāṃ| tilaiḥ
                        sayaṣṭīmadhukair vviśodhya sarppiḥ prayojyam madhurair vvipakvaṃ|| </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.12">
                        <label>4.18.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛteṣu doṣeṣu yathānupūrvvā granthau bhiṣak chleṣmasamutthiteṣu | svinnasya
                        vimlāpanam eva kuryād aṃguṣṭhaveṇudṛśadīsutais tu|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.13">
                        <label>4.18.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vikaṃkatāragvadhakākaṇantīkākādanītāpasavṛkṣamūlaiḥ| ālepayed enama
                        lāvubhārggīkarañjakālāmadanaiś ca vidvān|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.14">
                        <label>4.18.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         amarmmaje cānupa śīmymānasapakvam evāpahared vidārya| dahet sthite cāsṛji
                        siddhakarmmā sadyaḥ kṣatoktañ ca vidhim vidadhyāt|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.15">
                        <label>4.18.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yā māṃsakandyaḥ kaṭhinā bṛhatyastāsvapya yaṃ karmma vidhiḥ prayojyaḥ|
                        śastreṇa cāpāṭya vipakvamāśu prakṣālayet pathyatamaiḥ kaṣāyaiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.16">
                        <label>4.18.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃśodhanais tañ ca viśodhayīta kṣārottamaiḥ kṣaudraghṛtapragāḍhaiḥ| śuddhe
                        ca tailaṃ tvavacāraṇīyam viḍaṅgapāṭhārajanīvipakvaṃ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.17">
                        <label>4.18.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         medaḥsamutthe tilakalkadigdhaṃ tvacopariṣṭād dviguṇam paṭāntaṃ|
                        hutāśataptena muhuḥ pramṛjyā<unclear extent="1" unit="char"/>lena
                        dhīmānadahan hitāya|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.18">
                        <label>4.18.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pralipya dārvvīmatha lākṣayā vā prataptayā svedanam asya kāryaṃ| nipātya vā
                        śastramapohya medo dahet supakvan tv athavā vidārya|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.19">
                        <label>4.18.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣālya mūtraiś ca tilaiḥ supiṣṭaiḥ suvarccikādyair haritālamisraiḥ|
                        sasaindhavaiḥ kṣaudraghṛtapragāḍhaiḥ kṣārottarair enam abhipraśodhya|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.20">
                        <label>4.18.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ vidadyād dvikarañjaguñjāvaṅgāvalekheṅgudimūtrasiddhaiḥ| jīmūtakī
                        kośavatīphaleṣu dantī dravantī trivṛtāsu caiva|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.21">
                        <label>4.18.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarppiḥ kṛtaṃ hanty apacīṃ pravṛddhāṃ dvidhā pravṛttan tad udāravīryaṃ|
                        nirgguṇḍijātībarihiṣṭhayuktaṃ jīmūtakaṃ mākṣikasaindhavāḍhyaṃ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.22">
                        <label>4.18.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         abhiprataptaṃ vamanaṃ praśastaṃ duṣṭāpacīṣūttamamādiśanti| nirgguṇḍi
                        bimbīkaravīrasiddhaṃ tailaṃ hitaṃ śīrṣavirecanaṃ ca|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.23">
                        <label>4.18.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śākhoṭakalka svarasena siddhaṃ tailaṃ hitaṃ nasyaniśevanena| madhūkasāraś
                        ca hito vapīḍe phalāni śigroḥ kharamañjarervvā|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.24">
                        <label>4.18.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         granthīnamarmmaprabhavānapakvānuddhṛtya cāgniṃ vidadhīta vaidyaḥ| kṣāreṇa
                        cainaṃ pratisārayīt muhurmmhurllikhyama thoyathāvat|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.25">
                        <label>4.18.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pārṣṇim prati dvā daśa cāṅgulāni mātvendrabastim parivarjjya dhīmān|
                        vidārya matsyāṇḍanibhāni vaidyo jālāni niḥkramyavidhimviddhyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.26"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.27">
                        <label>4.18.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         maṇibandhopariṣṭādvā kuryād rekhātrayam bhiṣak| aṅgulāntaritaṃ samyag
                        apacīnāṃ nivṛttaye|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.28">
                        <label>4.18.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇṇasya kāle parcalākakākagodhāhikūrmmaprabhavās tumaṣyaḥ | dadyāc ca
                        tailena saheṅgudīnāṃ tailāni vakṣyāmi ca ślīpadeṣu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.29">
                        <label>4.18.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vairecanan dhūmam upādadīta bhavec ca nityaṃ yavamudgabhojī| karkkāruker
                        vvārukanālikerapiyālapañcāṅgulabījapūrṇṇaiḥ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.30">
                        <label>4.18.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātārbbudaṃ kṣīraghṛtāmbusiddhair uṣṇaiḥ satailair upanāhayettu| kuryāc ca
                        mukhyānuupanāhanārtham bhṛteṣu māṃseṣu ca veśavārāṃ|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.31">
                        <label>4.18.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svedam vidadhyāt kuśalantu nāḍyā śṛṅgena raktam bahuśo harecca|
                        vātaghnaniryūhapayomlabhāgaiḥ siddhaṃ śatākhya trivṛtam pibedvā|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.32">
                        <label>4.18.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svedopanāhā mṛduvas tu pathyāḥ pittārbbude kāyavirecanañ ca| vighṛṣya
                        codumbari kākagojīpatrairbhbhṛśaṃ kṣaudrayutaiḥ pralimpet|| </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.33">
                        <label>4.18.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sūkṣṇīkṛtaiḥ sarjjarasapriyaṃgūpattaṅgalodhrāñjanayaṣṭikāhvaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         visrāvya cāragvadhagojisomāḥ śyāmā va yojyāḥ kuśalena lepaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.34">
                        <label>4.18.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śyāmāgirihvārajanīraseṣu drākṣārase saptalikārase ca ||
                        <caesura/>
                         ghṛtaṃ pacet klītakajecasiddhaṃ pittārbudī tajjaṭhare ca jantuḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.35">
                        <label>4.18.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śuddhaś ca jantoḥ kaphaje rbude tu rakte 'vasikte ca tato 'rbudan tat |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkair ddihed ūrddhvamadhaś ca yani dravyāṇi doṣānapaciṃ nudanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.36">
                        <label>4.18.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kapotapārāvataviḍvimiśraiḥ sakāṃśanīlī śukalāṅgalākhyaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūlais tu kākādanimūlamisraiḥ kṣārapradigdhair athavā pradihyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.37">
                        <label>4.18.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         niṣpāvapiṇyākakulatthakalkair mmāṃsapragāḍhair ddadhimardditais tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         lepaṃ vidadhyāt krimayo yathātra mūrcchanti muñcanty atha makṣikā vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.38">
                        <label>4.18.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         alpāvaśiṣṭaṃ krimibhakṣitan tallikhettato 'gnim vidadhīta paścāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         yadalpamūlaṃ trapuśīsatāsrais tadveṣṭya paṭṭair athavāyasair vvā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.39">
                        <label>4.18.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣārāgniśastrāṇyavacārayīta muhur mmuhuḥ prāṇamahiṃsamānaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āsphotajātīkaravīrapatraiḥ kaṣāyam iṣṭaṃ vraṇaśodhanārthaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.40">
                        <label>4.18.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śuddhe ca tailaṃ vidadhīta bhārggīviḍaṅgapāṭhātriphalāsusiddhaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yadṛcchayā copagatāni pākaṃ krameṇa caivaopacaredvidhijñaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.41">
                        <label>4.18.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         medo 'rbbudaṃ svedya vidārya saudhya sīvyādyathoktaṃ gataraktamāśu |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato haridrāgṛhadhūmalodhrapattaṅgacūrṇṇaiḥ samanaḥ śilālaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.42">
                        <label>4.18.42</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇam pratigrāha madhupragāḍhaiḥ karañjatailaṃ vidadhīta śuddhe |
                        <caesura/>
                         saśeṣadoṣāṇi hi yo 'rbbudāni karoti tānyāśu punar bhbhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.43">
                        <label>4.18.43</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād aśeṣāṇi samuddharet tu hanyuḥ saśeṣāṇi yathā viṣāgnī |
                        <caesura/>
                         svinne 'nilothaṃ galagaṇḍamadau nāḍyāni laghnauṣadhapatrabhaṅgaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.44">
                        <label>4.18.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         amleṣu pattraiṣu payaḥ sucāpi svedaṃ vidaddhyāt piśiteṣu cāpi |
                        <caesura/>
                         visrāvayet svinnam atandritas tu rūḍhaṃ vraṇaṃ cāpy upanāhayīta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.45">
                        <label>4.18.45</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śaṇātasīmūlakeśigrusidgraiḥ piyālamajjāsahitais tilais tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         kālāmṛtāśigrupunarnnavārkkagajādināmākaraghāṭakuṣṭhaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.46">
                        <label>4.18.46</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ekaiṣikāvṛkṣakatilvakaiś ca surāmlapiṣṭaiḥ pradihedabhīkṣṇaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.47">
                        <label>4.18.47</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailam pibeccāmṛtavallinimbahansāhvayāvṛkṣakapippalībhiḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ balābhyāṃ sahadevadāru hitāya nityaṃ galagaṇḍaroge || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.48">
                        <label>4.18.48</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svedopanāhaiḥ kaphasambhavan tu saṃsvedaya visrāvaṇam eva kuryāt ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tato 'jagandhātiviṣāviśalyāviṣāṇikālāvuśukāñjānāśā kecit pāṭhahvayābhiḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.49">
                        <label>4.18.49</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         palāśabhasmodakapeśitābhir ddihyāt suguñjābhir aśītalābhiḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         daśārddhaśaṅkhair llavaṇaiś ca yuktaṃ tailaṃ pibetmāgadhikādisiddhaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.50">
                        <label>4.18.50</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         praccharddanaṃ śīrṣavirecanañ ca dhūpaś tu vair ecaniko hitas tu ||
                        <caesura/>
                         pākakramo vā pyanayo vidheyo vaidyena pākaṃgatayo kathañcit | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.51">
                        <label>4.18.51</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṭutrikakṣaudrayutāś ca śastā bhakṣyā yavānnāni rasāś ca maudgāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saśṛṃgaverāḥ sapaṭolanimbā hitāya deyā galagaṇḍaroge | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.52">
                        <label>4.18.52</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         medaḥsamutthe tu yathopadiṣṭāṃ vidhyet sirāṃ snigdhatanornnarasya ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śyāmāsudhālohapurīṣadantīrasāñjanaiś cāpi hitaḥ pralepaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.53">
                        <label>4.18.53</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtreṇa cāloḍya hitāya kalkaṃ prātaḥ pibet sāramahīruhāṇāṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śastreṇa vā 'pāṭya vidārite ca medaḥ samuddhṛtya hitāya sīvyet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.54">
                        <label>4.18.54</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         majjāvasākṣadrayutair ddahedvā dagdhe ca sarppirmmadhu cāvacāryaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsīsatutthe ca tato 'tra deye cūrṇṇīkṛte rocanayā ca yukte | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.18.55">
                        <label>4.18.55</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailena cābhyajya hitāya dadyāt sārodbhavaṃ gomayajañ ca bhasma |
                        <caesura/>
                         hitañ ca nityan triphalākaṣāyaṃ gā ḍhaś ca bandho yavabhojanañ ceti ||</l>
