                <div n="19" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 19]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.1"> athāto vṛddhyupadaṃśaślīpadānāṃ cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.3"> antravṛddhim ṛte ye 'nye vṛddhayas teṣu varjayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         vegāghātaṃ pṛṣṭhayānaṃ vyāyāmaṃ maithunaṃ tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.4"> anaśanaṃ cātyaśanam adhyaśanam atho guruḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrādito vātavṛddhau trivṛtāsnigdham āturam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.5"> sninnañ caiva yathānyāyam pāyayīta virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kośāmratilvakair aṇḍaphalatailāni vā naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.6"> sakṣīram vā pibet māsaṃ tailam eraṇḍasambhavaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ kāle 'nilaghnānāṃ kvāthaiḥ kalkaiś ca buddhimān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.7"> nirūhayen nirūḍhañ ca bhuktavantaṃ rasodanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaṣṭīmadhukasiddhena tatas tailena yojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.8"> svedopanāhau kuryāc ca pradehām̐ś cānilāpahān |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidagdham pācayitvā vā sevanīm parivarjjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.9"> bhindyād bhitvā ca matimān yathoktaṃ kramam ācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittagranthikramaṅ kuryād apakvam pittasambhave || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.10"> śastropapannam bhitvā vā śodhayen madhusarppiṣā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuddhe ca copaśaṅ kalkaṃ dadyāt tailan tu yaddhitaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.11"> muhur muhur jjalaukābhiḥ śoṇitaṃ raktaje haret |
                        <caesura/>
                         pibed virecanam vāpi śarkkarākṣaudrasaṃyutaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.12"> pittagranthikramaṃ kuryād āme pakve ca raktaje |
                        <caesura/>
                         śleṣmavṛddhim uṣṇavīryair mmūtrapiṣṭais tu lepayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.13"> pītadārukaṣāyañ ca pibet mūtreṇa saṃyutaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vimlāpanād ṛte cāpi śleṣmagranthikrame hitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.14"> pakvabhinne viśuddhyarthan tailaṃ deyam vijānatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sumanāruṣkarāṅkoṭhasaptaparṇṇeṣu sādhitaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.15"> svedyam medaḥ samutthan tu lepayet surasādinā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirekadravyair vvā sukhoṣṇair mmūtrasaṃyutaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.16"> svinnam vāveṣṭa paṭṭena samāśvāsya ca mānavaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣamūlaṃ sevanīñ ca vṛddhipattreṇa dārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.17"> medaḥ samuddhṛtya tato dadyāt kāsīsasaindhave |
                        <caesura/>
                         badhnīyāc ca yathoddiṣṭaṃ śuddhe tailañ ca dāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.18"> manaḥśilālalavaṇaiḥ siddhamāruḥkareṣu ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedyamūtranimittan tu vastrapaṭṭena veṣṭayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.19"> sevanyām pārśvato 'dhastād vidhyed vrīhimukhena vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         athātrodaravan nāḍīn dattvā visrāvayed bhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.20"> mūtranāḍīm athoddhṛtya sthavikābandham ācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuddhe ca ropaṇan dadyād varjjayed antrahaitukaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.19.21"> aprāptaphalakose vā vātavṛddhikramo hitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                <div n="20" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 20]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.1">
                        <label>4.20.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ kṣudrarogāṇā cikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.3">
                        <label>4.20.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrādita eva jagañ jalāyukābhir grāhayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkaiś cālepayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.4">
                        <label>4.20.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śyāmāpāṭhālāṅgalīkalkair vā pakvām vā pākavidhānenopacaret ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.5-6">
                        <label>4.20.5-6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yavaprakhyām ambālajīṃ panasikām pāṣāṇagardabhaṅ kacchapikāñ ca svedayitvā
                        suradārukuṣṭhaharitālamanaḥśilākalkair ālepayet | pakvāṃ vā
                        pākavidhānenopacaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.7-8">
                        <label>4.20.7-8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vivṛtām indraviddhāṃ gardabhikāṃ jālagardabham irivellikāṃ gandhanāmāṃ
                        kakṣām visphoṭāṃś ca pittavisarpavidhānenopacaret | pakvāṃś ca
                        madhurauṣadhasiddhena sarpiṣā ropayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.9-10">
                        <label>4.20.9-10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         cipyān tūṣṇāmbunā pariṣecyotkṛtyāpanayec cakratailenābhyajya
                        sarjarasarasacūrṇṇenāvacūrṇṇya bandhenopacared evam aśakyam agninā dahet |
                        madhurauṣadhasiddhena ca tailenopacaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.11">
                        <label>4.20.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         anuśayīṃ śleṣma vidradhivad upacaret | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.12-13">
                        <label>4.20.12-13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vidārikām abhyajya parisvedya vimlāpayet |
                        bilvamūlanāgavṛttikāvarṣābhūkalkaiś cālepayet | vraṇabhāvaṇam āpannaṃ vā
                        madhurakaṣāyauṣadhasiddhena tailena ropayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.14"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.15"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.16"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.17-18">
                        <label>4.20.17-18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śarkarārbudam medorbudavad upacaret ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kacchūvicarcikārakaśāsu kuṣṭhavat pratīkāro viśeṣatas tu
                        śatāhvāsarṣapakalkair ālepayet | siddhārthakadāruharidrākalkair vā |
                        saralātailena vā | kaṭukauṣadhasiddhenābhyañjyāt | naktamālatailena vā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.19">
                        <label>4.20.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pakvāṃś ca pakvavidhānenopacaret ||
                        <caesura/>
                         pādadāryān tu sirām vidhyet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.20">
                        <label>4.20.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pādau snehasvedopapannā madhūcchiṣṭaghṛtavasāmajjābhir yavakṣāramiśrair
                        ālepayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.21-22">
                        <label>4.20.21-22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         alase tv āmlakāñjikasiktau caraṇau paṭolapicumardatilakāsīsarocanākalkair
                        ālepayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.23">
                        <label>4.20.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nidigdhikārasasiddhena ca sarṣapatailenābhyajya
                        kāsīsarocanāmanaḥśilācūrṇṇaiḥ pratisārayet || kadaram uddhṛtya dahet snehena
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.24">
                        <label>4.20.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         indralupte tu śirasi sirām vidhā tu ndamanaḥśilāmaricakalkair ālepayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.25-26">
                        <label>4.20.25-26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhadradārukalkair vā jātīcitrakakaravīranaktamālakalkasiddhena
                        tailenābhyañjyāt | rasāyanavidhānañ cāsevena | avagāḍhapadaṃ pracchayitvā
                        guñjāphalakalkair bhūyo bhūyaḥ pradihyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.27-29">
                        <label>4.20.27-29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śoṇitam avasicya nimbodakena parisicyāśvaviḍrasena lavaṇapragāḍhenālepayet
                        | paṭolapicumardaharidrākalkair vā | madhukotpalatilairaṇḍamārkavapatrair vā
                        | indraluptoktena tailenābhyañjyāt || dāruṇake tu snigdhasvinnasya lalāṭe
                        sirām vyadhet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.30">
                        <label>4.20.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         avapīḍaśiro bastyabhyagāś cāseveta | kodravatṛṇakṣaraudakaprakṣālanañ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.31a">
                        <label>4.20.31a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         palitaprakāram anyatra vakṣyāmaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.31b-32a">
                        <label>4.20.31b-32a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         masūrikāṃ kaphapittavisarpakuṣṭhaharapralepanādikriyām upadiśanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.32b-33a">
                        <label>4.20.32b-33a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jatumaṇimaśakacarmakīlatilakālakāṃs tu śastreṇotkṛtya kṣāreṇa pratisārayet
                        | agninā vā dahet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.33">
                        <label>4.20.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nacchanīlikāvyaṅgeṣu yathābhyāśaṃ lalāṭe sirām visrāvayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.34">
                        <label>4.20.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīravṛkṣakalkaiś ca kṣīrapiṣṭair avaghṛṣyālepayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.35">
                        <label>4.20.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         balātibalāmadhukaharidrākalkair vā | suvarṇṇagairikāgurupayasyākalkair vā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.36">
                        <label>4.20.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         taruṇakapittharājādanakalkair vā | sūkaradaṃṣṭrayā vā madhughṛtayuktayā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.37-38a">
                        <label>4.20.37-38a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yūnām api yuvān api akāsv eṣa eva vidhiḥ | viśeṣatas tu pracchardanam iṣṭam
                        ālepaś ca siddhārthakavacālodhrasaindhavakalkair vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.38i"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.38ii"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.38b-39a">
                        <label>4.20.38b-39a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         padminīkaṇṭake tu nimbodakavāntasya nimbodakasarpiḥ kṣaudram pātum
                        prayacchet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.39b">
                        <label>4.20.39b</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nimbāragvadhakaṣāyaṃ cotsādane || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.40-41">
                        <label>4.20.40-41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         parivarttikāṃ tu sarpiṣābhyajya svedayet | vātaghnais tataḥ sninnām
                        upanāhayet | sālvalena veśavāreṇa vā trirātram pañcarātram vā tataḥ
                        svedayitvābhyajya śanaiḥ śanaiś carma samānayaṃ manipatham avapīḍayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.42">
                        <label>4.20.42</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pariveṣṭitañ ca punar upanāhayet | nityañ ca snigdham annam āharet ||
                        avapāṭikayām apy evaṃ yathādoṣaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.43">
                        <label>4.20.43</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         niruddhaprakāśe tu suvarṇṇādīnāṃ nāḍīm ubhayatomukhīṃ dāruvīm vā jatuvṛtāṃ
                        sarpiṣābhyajya srotasi | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.44">
                        <label>4.20.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         praṇidhāya śiśumāravasāvarāhamajjābhiḥ pariṣecayec cakratailena vāt |
                        surabhivacadevadārusiddhena | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.45">
                        <label>4.20.45</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tryahāt tryahāc ca sthūlatarīṃ nāḍīm praṇidadhyād evam asya srotodvāraṃ
                        varddhayet | snigdhañ cāhāram upaseveta | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.46a">
                        <label>4.20.46a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śastreṇa vā sevanīṃ vimucyāvadārayet | tataḥ sadya kṣatavad upācaret | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.46b-47a">
                        <label>4.20.46b-47a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         agnirohiṇīṃ sanniruddhagudaṃ valmīkañ ca pratyākhyāyopacaret | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.47b">
                        <label>4.20.47b</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         visarpoktena vidhānenāgnirohiṇīṃ cikitset | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.48a">
                        <label>4.20.48a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sanniruddhagudaṃ niruddhaprakaśavat | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.48b-49">
                        <label>4.20.48b-49</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         valmīkaṃ śastreṇotkṛtyāgnikṣārābhyām upacaret tataḥ saṃśodhya ropayed
                        arbudavidhāṇena || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.50"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.51"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.57-58a">

                        <caesura/>
                        <handShift/>ahipūtane dhātryāḥ stanyaṃ śodheta | bālasya
                        triphalārasāṃjanapaṭolaiḥ siddhaṃ sarpiḥ pānam iṣṭaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.58b">

                        <caesura/>
                         triphalākhadirabadarīkaṣāyam vraṇaśodhanaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.59">
                        <label>4.20.59</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsīsarocanātutthaharitālarasāñjanair amlapiṣṭaiḥ pralepanaṃ |
                        badaracūrṇṇair vā saindhavamiśraiḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.60">
                        <label>4.20.60</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇṇakāle tu cūrṇṇaḥ kapālatutthajaḥ || vṛṣaṇakacchvām pāmāvad upacāro
                        hipūtanavac ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.61">
                        <label>4.20.61</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gudabhraṃśe tu gudaṃ svedyasnehenābhyajya praveśya praviṣṭe ca svedaṃ
                        kuryād uccāranirgamanārthaṃ | chidreṇa cāsya carmaṇā kaupīnabandhaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.62">
                        <label>4.20.62</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ cāsya pānābhyañjanārtham vipacet | mūṣikaṃ niraṃtraṃ kalpayitvā
                        mahāpañcamūlakṣīram vipacet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.20.63">
                        <label>4.20.63</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatas tasmiṃ tailam vātaharakalkaprativāpam vipaced etat kṛcchram api
                        gudatraṃ saṃsādhayateti ||</l>
